{"answers": ["The vascular cambium", "the vascular cambium"], "model_answer": "According to the provided documents, secondary xylem and phloem cells arise from the vascular cambium. The vascular cambium is responsible for the secondary growth of plants, which is the growth that occurs after the primary growth stage."}

{"answers": ["at birth", "birth"], "model_answer": "According to the provided documents, closure of the ductus arteriosus occurs at birth, during the first few days of life. The ductus arteriosus is a blood vessel that connects the pulmonary artery to the aorta in the fetus, allowing blood to bypass the lungs and oxygenate the body through the placenta. After birth, the ductus arteriosus closes, and the pulmonary circulation becomes established, allowing the lungs to take over the job of oxygenating the blood."}

The federal government had limited powers, such as declaring war, making treaties, and appointing ambassadors, but it did not have the power to levy taxes, regulate commerce, or enforce laws.
